              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8096484-jessica-the-psychotic-nerd?shelf=the-afterlife">the-afterlife</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8096484-jessica-the-psychotic-nerd?shelf=ghosts-and-such">ghosts-and-such</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer370245519" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13995964649744467219">This and other reviews can be found on <a href='http://thepsychoticnerd.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Psychotic Nerd</a> <br/><br/>Actual Rating: 3.5 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Thoughts</u>
</b><br/>For some reason, I find books about the afterlife interesting. This book isn't quite about the afterlife, but it has been sitting in the TBR pile for a long time and I'm surprised that I hadn't picked it up until now. <br/><br/>The book focuses on Elizabeth. On the morning of her eighteenth birthday, Elizabeth wakes to find that she's dead, her body fallen over the side of the yacht. She doesn't remember how s</span>
  <span id="freeText13995964649744467219" style="display:none">This and other reviews can be found on <a href="http://thepsychoticnerd.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">The Psychotic Nerd</a> <br /><br />Actual Rating: 3.5 Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <u>My Thoughts</u>
</b><br />For some reason, I find books about the afterlife interesting. This book isn't quite about the afterlife, but it has been sitting in the TBR pile for a long time and I'm surprised that I hadn't picked it up until now. <br /><br />The book focuses on Elizabeth. On the morning of her eighteenth birthday, Elizabeth wakes to find that she's dead, her body fallen over the side of the yacht. She doesn't remember how she died or even the last few months of her life. Her death seems like an accident, but Elizabeth isn't sure. With the help of another ghost, Alex, Elizabeth tries to remember her life up until her death. <br /><br />Elizabeth was a hard character to understand at first. She's pretty, popular, and rich. Her personality sometimes came out bratty and I found her a bit frustrating. As the story continued, I grew to understand Elizabeth's character and what exactly was going on in her mind leading up to her death. <br /><br />This book is interesting because even though it has paranormal elements, such as having someone walk on earth after their death and entering their memories, this book was also a mystery. The mystery was also surprising for the most part. There were a few elements I guessed ahead of time, even though I wished they weren't true, but there was also enough to keep me guessing.<br /><br />This book gets very dark and emotional. This was to be expected since it deals with death, but it also dealt with other tough subjects such as guilt, blackmail, mental health, etc. It was very hard reading this book as it got closer to the end because even though Elizabeth got on my nerves at first when I started to understand what she went through, I had to realize that no matter what, Elizabeth is dead and did not get a happy end in life. Alex didn't get a happy end in life either, but gosh, I can't even articulate how much change he went through.<br /><br /><u>
  <b>IN CONCLUSION</b>
</u><br />I thought this was an interesting read. I'm not sure what prevented me from giving this book 4 stars. While I thought this was a very interesting, albeit dark, read, I think part of my misgivings with Elizabeth in the beginning, as well as parts of the end (which felt off), affected my rating. I do think that this book is worth a read. I have not read any other books by Warman, but I may need to read more from this author in the future.</span>

<div id="review_737108056" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737108056" />
    <a title="Eilonwy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17237503-eilonwy"><img alt="Eilonwy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1506803497p2/17237503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737108056?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eilonwy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eilonwy" href="/user/show/17237503-eilonwy">Eilonwy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17237503-eilonwy?shelf=fast-paced">fast-paced</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17237503-eilonwy?shelf=heartbreaking">heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17237503-eilonwy?shelf=heartwarming">heartwarming</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17237503-eilonwy?shelf=tear-jerking">tear-jerking</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737108056" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13811533498261967465"><blockquote>In the middle of the night on Elizabeth Valchar's eighteenth birthday, she is awakened by a strange thumping sound. When she finds the source of the sound, she realizes that nothing will ever be the same again. But how did things GET to this point? Through a mix of the present and the past, she and the reader solve two mysteries and try to find a sense of closure. </blockquote>I'm not sure what to say about this book. It was fast-paced and gripping; I barely put it down until I finished it. But ... despite a</span>
  <span id="freeText13811533498261967465" style="display:none"><blockquote>In the middle of the night on Elizabeth Valchar's eighteenth birthday, she is awakened by a strange thumping sound. When she finds the source of the sound, she realizes that nothing will ever be the same again. But how did things GET to this point? Through a mix of the present and the past, she and the reader solve two mysteries and try to find a sense of closure. </blockquote>I'm not sure what to say about this book. It was fast-paced and gripping; I barely put it down until I finished it. But ... despite a certain poignancy, it's left me feeling vaguely icky and unclean now that I have finished it. I don't know if it's just me, because I often feel this way after watching an episode of, say, "Law and Order," or finishing a murder mystery (which this book essentially is). There's just something about seeing the worst side of people, especially when it leads to tragedy, that makes me profoundly uncomfortable.<br /><br />The book is well-written, and the characters mostly rang true and more than one-dimensional to me. Liz and her friends are the ultra-popular crowd at her school, good-looking, rich, and mean -- more feared than genuinely liked. But Liz's interior life isn't nearly so good as her exterior would lead one to believe, and that's where the tension of the story is to be found. The mismatch between her two selves is portrayed well, and I did believe in her development over the course of the story as the author provided more and more snippets of information. It had some similarities to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6482837.Before_I_Fall" title="Before I Fall by Lauren Oliver" rel="nofollow noopener">Before I Fall</a> in character, story arc, and even the writing style, but it's definitely its own book. I really don't want to say too much in case anyone else might want to read the story.<br /><br />So ... this was a cracking good read, but be warned that there is no feel-good at the end of this book. Read at your own risk.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13811533498261967465" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_903773571" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/903773571" />
    <a title="Aishwarya Rao" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5832812-aishwarya-rao"><img alt="Aishwarya Rao" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585389794p2/5832812.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/903773571?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aishwarya Rao" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aishwarya Rao" href="/user/show/5832812-aishwarya-rao">Aishwarya Rao</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer903773571" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer277436447620881083"> I haven't written a review in what seems like forever, so I may be little rusty.<br/> Let me start off by saying that I having once been a book worm, I haven't so much as touched a book in over a year. So I think Im in a suitable position to say that Im absolutely glad to have started off once more with Between.<br/>Jessica Warman is becoming one of my favorite authors of all time. Her books are mysterious and haunting. They leave you feeling tingly and confused but at the same time satisfied. <br/>Between wa</span>
  <span id="freeText277436447620881083" style="display:none"> I haven't written a review in what seems like forever, so I may be little rusty.<br /> Let me start off by saying that I having once been a book worm, I haven't so much as touched a book in over a year. So I think Im in a suitable position to say that Im absolutely glad to have started off once more with Between.<br />Jessica Warman is becoming one of my favorite authors of all time. Her books are mysterious and haunting. They leave you feeling tingly and confused but at the same time satisfied. <br />Between was exuberating. <br />The character of Elizabeth is slightly disturbing and kind of ruthless and prissy, but I loved how she had a deeper character beneath her self centered surface. Richie, again, a character with two sides is a character which I adored. I think Jessica Warman was trying to instill a very vital message through her character, No One is Perfect. Every character, from Liz, her mother, her father, Richie, their friends, even Richie's parents are flawed. Unlike usual young adult book, the male lead role isn't portrayed as "Perfect". This gives the book a more believable and relatable aura. <br /><br />The story line was exhilarating. I found the concept, and plot brilliant though I felt that the writing style wasn't as captivating and had scope for improvement (hence only 4 stars). I found the book slightly boring in the beginning, also I was able to predict the plot from <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when she has the flashback of visiting Vince for help with her car  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I also felt that the relationship between Liz and Alex could have been developed a little more. I didn't feel like their was any kind of connection or any feeling of understanding between the two, even towards the end of the book.<br /><br />On the whole, the book is pleasing. It leaves you with a haunting sensation. After I read the last few pages I had a sudden craving to have a bath. Also, I shed a few tears *sigh*. <br />As soon as I read this book, one thing was clear. I want to read MORE Jessica Warman.</span>
  <a data-text-id="277436447620881083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13224242508060869119">Thanks to teenreads.com I received a very early sneak peek copy of Jessica Warman's upcoming book Between. <br/><br/>In return I had to fill out a questionnaire with my reaction to the book. I'm not sure if there will be changes made to the book prior to its release later this year. If there are I'm sure they will be minor.<br/><br/>Since I don't want to give out any spoilers I'm just going to say this book is well written and drew me into the story from the first chapter. There is some content that would make me h</span>
  <span id="freeText13224242508060869119" style="display:none">Thanks to teenreads.com I received a very early sneak peek copy of Jessica Warman's upcoming book Between. <br /><br />In return I had to fill out a questionnaire with my reaction to the book. I'm not sure if there will be changes made to the book prior to its release later this year. If there are I'm sure they will be minor.<br /><br />Since I don't want to give out any spoilers I'm just going to say this book is well written and drew me into the story from the first chapter. There is some content that would make me hesitate to recommend it to conservative readers. I liked the mystery element to this book and it's not until the very end that the pieces of the puzzle all come together. Often I know exactly where a book is going. I did figure out much of the story early on but there were enough twists and turns to keep me wondering.<br /><br />The characters in this book are nothing like me but I could still relate to them and the struggles they were going through. The teen characters and their parents were very flawed and made many poor choices. I enjoyed this book despite the content I could have done without.<br /><br />Between will be released in August or September of 2011.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicawarman.com/2011/02/sneak-peek-at-between/">http://jessicawarman.com/2011/02/snea...</a> <br /><br />Content: Without giving away any spoilers I would say this book is not for younger teens. There is a lots of content: drinking, drugs, smoking, language (including a half dozen F words), talk of sex (although no sex scene) and topics too mature for a younger audience. <br /><br />Rating: 4 Stars<br /><br />Source: Sneak Peek received via teenreads.com</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer195424955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2491082711798929889">This book is definitely disturbing, but it's also one of the only mysteries that has held my attention up the very end. <br/><br/>I wanted to read this story way past my bedtime, it was such a page-turner. It really wasn't until there were only 100 pages left that realization started to hit and I was able to put most of the pieces together.<br/><br/>Sometimes the drug use got a little old. The book had a wishy-washy stance on whether drugs are bad or just something the cool kids do. It was was also hard to read abo</span>
  <span id="freeText2491082711798929889" style="display:none">This book is definitely disturbing, but it's also one of the only mysteries that has held my attention up the very end. <br /><br />I wanted to read this story way past my bedtime, it was such a page-turner. It really wasn't until there were only 100 pages left that realization started to hit and I was able to put most of the pieces together.<br /><br />Sometimes the drug use got a little old. The book had a wishy-washy stance on whether drugs are bad or just something the cool kids do. It was was also hard to read about all of Liz's parents' marital problems. It's sad to see a teenager having to worry about such an adult drama.<br /><br />I really don't want to go into a lot of detail in my review because I want anyone who reads it to be able to uncover all of the subtle hints gradually like i did.<br /><br />I always think it's interesting to see that even the "popular" kids at school have many layers and facets to their personalities, with many reasons that they act the way they do. The author did a great job of showing all the layers of Liz's life. She might not have been so likable at first glance, until learning about her life throughout the book.<br /><br />Overall, a dark, tragic look at what can lie beneath the surface.<br /><br /><br />ARC sent by publisher in exchange for honest review<br /><br />reviewed for <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://inthehammockblog.blogspot.com">http://inthehammockblog.blogspot.com</a><br /><br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Nrcml/5ixbWuIXTWWpuOqWEoOT58rNzbQz5yWJzrbB4Nu70n6R3Zp4wC4Oi5h2bTSwOfbpdpEPCL4SxxI0AQgw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('CeXQJH42xzHkE55Ke3n+5KU9zg8DUyuTpRcUylhuMW8y6UuUaUnbI8YwCnSYZRaejxZoX+iW57htyErj58VN8g==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/2921810.Jessica_Warman">About Jessica Warman</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/2921810.Jessica_Warman"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_111x148-8060b12280b2aec7543bafb574ee8422.png);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/2921810.Jessica_Warman">Jessica Warman
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__followerCount'>
369
followers
</div>

</div>
</div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15732216728868696049">Jessica Warman is the author of Breathless, which received three starred reviews and was an ALA Best Book for Young Adults, and Where the Truth Lies. The idea for Between came from an incident in her childhood, when a local boy went missing after a party on a yacht (he was eventually found, alive).</span>

</div>
</div>
